NOTIFICATIONS  BY  GOVERNMENT
II-2 Ex. (143)
[ 1 ]
INDUSTRIES DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS.
FORM IV
PRELIMINARY NOTIFICATION
Unit IV, Block 1-10
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 121, ªî£N™ (Täâ‹) ¶¬ø, 26 HŠóõK 2021, 
ñ£C 14, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´&2052.]
No. II(2)/IND/132(v-1)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 217.04.90 hectares of land is 
required in the Padukkapathu Village in Sathankulam Taluk in Thoothukudi District for public purpose, 
namely establishing a new launch station for SSLV and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Since the land is urgently required under sub-section (1) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair 
Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement (RFCTLARR) Act 
2013, involving ISRO/Defence of India under sub-section (2) of Section 40 of the said Act, it has been 
decided not to carry out the Social Impact Assessment Study vide G.O. (Ms.) No.175 Industries (GIM) 
Department dated 09-10-2019.
No families are likely to be displaced due to the acquisition of 112.33.30 hectares of lands in Block-1 
to 10 of Unit IV in Padukkapathu Village for the above said project.  In anyway the Deputy Collector, 
Thoothukudi (Oﬃ  ce at Tiruchendur) is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of rehabilitation and 
resettlement of the aﬀ ected families.     
 Therefore, it is notiﬁ ed that for the above said project in the Padukkapathu Village of Sathankulam 
Taluk in Thoothukudi District, land measuring an extent of 112.33.30 hectares, whose details are speciﬁ ed 
in the Schedule below is under acquisition in Block –1 to 10 of Unit IV.

6.32.90
This notiﬁ cation is made under sub-section (1) of Section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement 
Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) to all whom it may concern.
A plan of the lands may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer, (Land Acquisition) SSLV Project, Tiruchendur 
on any working day during the working hours.
The Government is pleased to authorize the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur and his staﬀ  to enter upon a survey land, 
take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work as provided and speciﬁ ed in section 12 of the said Act.
Under sub-section (4) of section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land i.e. sale/purchase, etc., or create any 
encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this notiﬁ cation in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette without prior approval of the Collector.
In view of urgency of the case, the provision of hearing of objections under section 15 of the said Act is dispensed with and in view of urgency of the 
case is become necessary to acquire immediate possession of the land speciﬁ ed in the schedule under the provision of the sub section (1) of section 40 of 
the said Act.   
        
 
N. MURUGANANDAM,
Principal Secretary to Government.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
FORM IV
[SEE RULE 16 ]
PRELIMINERY NOTIFICATION
UNIT-V, Block 1-12
[G.O.Ms. No. 122, Industries (GIM), 26th February 2021, ñ£C 14, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´&2052]
No. II(2)/IND/132(V-2)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 677.30.55 hectares of land is required in the Madhavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur 
Taluk, in Thoothukudi District for public purpose, namely establishing a new launch Station for SSLV and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Since the land is urgently required under sub-section (1) of Section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation 
and Resettlement (RFCTLARR) Act 2013, involving ISRO/Defence of India under sub-section (2) of Section 40 of the said Act, it has been decided not to carry 
out the Social Impact Assessment Study vide G.O. (Ms) No.175, Industries (GIM) Department dated 09-10-2019.
No families are likely to be displaced due to the acquisition of 113.25.50 hectares of lands in Block-1 to 12 of Unit V in Madhavankurichi village for 
the above said project. In anyway the Deputy Collector, Thoothukudi (Oﬃ  ce at Tiruchendur) is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of rehabilitation and 
resettlement of the aﬀ ected families.     
Therefore, it is notiﬁ ed that for the above said project in the Madhavankurichi Village of Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District, land measuring an extent 
of 113.25.50 hectares, whose details are speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below is under acquisition in Block – 1 to 12 of Unit V.

This notiﬁ cation is made under Sub-section (1) of Section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and 
Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) to all whom it may concern.
A plan of the lands may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer, (Land Acquisition) SSLV Project, 
Tiruchendur on any working day during the working hours.
 
The Government is pleased to authorize the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur and his staﬀ  to enter upon 
a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work as provided and 
speciﬁ ed in section 12 of the said Act.
 
Under Sub-section (4) of Section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land i.e. sale/purchase, etc., 
or create any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this notiﬁ cation in the  Tamil Nadu Government Gazette without prior approval of 
the Collector.
 
In view of urgency of the case, the provision of hearing of objections under Section 15 of the said Act is dispensed with and in view of urgency of 
the case is become necessary to acquire immediate possession of the land speciﬁ ed in the schedule under the provision of the sub section (1) of Section 
40 of the said Act.   
N. MURUGANANDAM,
Principal Secretary to Government.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
FORM IV
PRELIMINARY NOTIFICATION
(UNIT-VI, Block 1-11)
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 123, ªî£N™ (Täâ‹) ¶¬ø, 26 HŠóõK 2021, 
ñ£C 14, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´&2052]
No. II(2)/IND/132(V-3)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 677.30.55 hectares of land is required in the Madhavankurichi Village in Tiruchendur 
Taluk in Thoothukudi District for public purpose, namely establishing a new launch station for SSLV and for formation of a new road to re-route the ECR.
Since the land is urgently required under sub-section (1) of section 40 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation 
and Resettlement (RFCTLARR)  Act 2013,  involving ISRO/Defence of India under sub-section (2) of section 40 of the said Act, it has been decided not to 
carry out  the Social Impact Assessment Study vide G.O.(Ms) No.175 Industries (GIM) Department dated 09.10.2019.
No families are likely to be displaced due to the acquisition of 110.96.34 hectares of lands in Block-1 to 11 of Unit VI in Madhavankurichi village for 
the above said project. In anyway the Deputy Collector, Thoothukudi (Oﬃ  ce at Tiruchendur) is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of rehabilitation and 
resettlement of the aﬀ ected families.     
 Therefore, it is notiﬁ ed that for the above said project in Madhavankurichi village of Tiruchendur Taluk in Thoothukudi District, land measuring an extent 
of 110.96.34  hectares, whose details are speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below is under acquisition in Block-1 to 11 of Unit VI.

This notiﬁ cation is made under sub-section (1) of section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and 
Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013) to all whom it may concern.
A plan of the lands may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Collector, Thoothukudi and the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer, (Land Acquisition) SSLV Project, 
Tiruchendur on any working day during the working hours.
 
The Government is pleased to authorize the Special District Revenue Oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), SSLV Project, Tiruchendur and his staﬀ  to enter upon 
a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work as provided and 
speciﬁ ed in section 12 of the said Act.
 
Under sub-section (4) of section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land i.e. sale/purchase, etc., 
or create any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this notiﬁ cation in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette without prior approval of the 
Collector.
 
In view of urgency of the case, the provision of hearing of objections under section 15 of the said Act is dispensed with and in view of urgency of 
the case is become necessary to acquire immediate possession of the land speciﬁ ed in the schedule under the provision of the sub section (1) of section 40 
of the said Act.   
.   
N. MURUGANANDAM,
Principal Secretary to Government.
